| <span data-ttu-id="83cb5-815">Voce</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="83cb5-815">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="83cb5-816">Valore</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="83cb5-816">Value</span></span> |
